   21| 	Kf = 0.591      																					{Thermal conductivity of water                 	[W/m/K]}
   22|     kx=1																								{horizontal k value}{m/d}
   23| {Sediment properties}
   24| 	T0= 25			 																			{average background temperature at T=0}
   25|     inflowTemp=T0
   26| 	n = 0.41																								{porositiy}
   27| 	rhos = 2650 																						{Density sediment} {kg/m3}
   28| 	cs=830																								{Specific head sediment}{J/kg*K}
   29| 	Ks = {2.3}5{7.59}      																			{Thermal conductivity of solid particles   [W/m/K]}
   30| 
   31| {Combined properties}
   32| 	cb=n*rhow*cw+(1-n)*rhos*cs														{Combined specific head}{J/{m**3*K}}
   33| 	Kb=	(n*Kf)+((1-n)*Ks) 																	{Combined thermal conductivity}{J/{m*sec*K}}
   34| 	qx=(-kx/tday)*dx(head)																	{flux in x direction}
   35| 	qy=(-kx/tday)*dy(head)																	{flux in y direction}
   36| 	q=vector(qx,qy)																				{combined flux}
   37| 	Source=0
   38|

   42|     t_cutoff = 1800										{time till heating turns off}
   43|     t_transition = 2											{short transition time from full heat to zero}

  132| {--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------HEATING INPUT CALCULATION-----------------------------------------------------------------}
  133| 
  134| {Calculation of  heating by the core of the heating cable}
  135| 	A_heating=pi*Rad_heat_core^2 																			{Cross-sectional area of heating part      										[m^2]}
  136| 	!HK {Q_heating=((Cableheat^2)/(R_heat_core*L_heat_core))/L_heat_core}								{Calculated heat input for the cable}
  137| 	!Q_heating=(1-exp(-t/10))*((Cableheat^2)/(R_heat_core*L_heat_core))/L_heat_core								{Calculated heat input for the cable}
  138|     
  139|     Q_heating = (1 - exp(-t / t_transition)) *
  140|     					(Cableheat^2 / (R_heat_core * L_heat_core^2)) *
  141|     					(1 / (1 + exp(min((t - t_cutoff) / t_transition, 690))))
  142| 
  143| {----------------------------------------Cable orientation 1 / location A3}
  144| {Centre location}
  145| 	Locx_A3=0
  146| 	Locy_A3=0
  147| {Strenght cable}
  148| 	Locx_A3_SC = Locx_A3
  149| 	Locy_A3_SC = Locy_A3
  150| {DTS cables}
  151| 	Locx_A3_DTS1 = Locx_A3+Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO		{DTS right side}
  152| 	Locy_A3_DTS1 = Locy_A3
  153| 	Locx_A3_DTS2 = Locx_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*cos(90*(pi/180)))		{DTS Top side}
  154| 	Locy_A3_DTS2 = Locy_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*sin(90*(pi/180)))	
  155| 	Locx_A3_DTS3 = Locx_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*cos(180*(pi/180)))		{DTS Left side}
  156| 	Locy_A3_DTS3 = Locy_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*sin(180*(pi/180)))	
  157| 	Locx_A3_DTS4 = Locx_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*cos(270*(pi/180)))		{DTS bottom side}
  158| 	Locy_A3_DTS4 = Locy_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*sin(270*(pi/180)))

  165| 	Locy_A3_heat3=Locy_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*sin(150*(pi/180)))
  166| 	Locx_A3_heat4=Locx_A3+((Rad_Strenght_Mantle+Rad_DTS_TPEO)*cos(240*(pi/180))) {bottom left}

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. 
<Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. 
<Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral (eg, <Vb.x>) represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function.
'tri3', 'tet20', etc., represents a basis function in the indicated basis.
The operator <S.c> represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.
